#WESTERN AESTHETIC#

#Basilical Art
MA_basilical_secular_01 = { #Secular
	type_icon = "MA_basilical_secular.dds"
	cost_gold = normal_building_tier_1_cost
	construction_time = standard_construction_time
	next_building = MA_basilical_secular_02
	can_construct_potential = {
		has_building_or_higher = castle_01
		required_innovation = { INNOVATION = basilical_art }
	}
	can_construct = { required_innovation = { INNOVATION = motte } }
	is_enabled = { scope:holder.capital_province = this }
	on_complete = {
		MA_medium_development_increase_effect = yes
		MA_medium_prestige_increase_effect = yes
		#Heavenly Vault perk
		MA_heavenly_vault_renown_effect = yes
	}
	character_modifier = {
		direct_vassal_opinion = 3
		monthly_prestige_gain_mult = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
	}
	max_garrison = normal_building_max_garrison_tier_1
	province_modifier = {
		monthly_income = normal_building_tax_tier_1
	}
	county_modifier = {
		tax_mult = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
		levy_size = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
	}
	ai_value = {
		base = 15
	}
}

MA_basilical_religious_01 = { #Religious
	type_icon = "MA_basilical_religious.dds"
	cost_gold = normal_building_tier_1_cost
	construction_time = standard_construction_time
	next_building = MA_basilical_religious_02
	can_construct_potential = {
		has_building_or_higher = castle_01
		required_innovation = { INNOVATION = basilical_art }
	}
	can_construct = { required_innovation = { INNOVATION = crop_rotation } }
	is_enabled = { required_religion = { RELIGION = christianity } is_county_capital = yes }
	on_complete = {
		MA_medium_development_increase_effect = yes
		MA_medium_piety_increase_effect = yes
		MA_patronage_perk_3_bonus = { TIER = 1 }
	}
	character_modifier = {
		clergy_opinion = 3
		monthly_piety_gain_mult = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
	}
	province_modifier = {
		build_speed = normal_building_build_speed_tier_1
		monthly_income = normal_building_tax_tier_1
	}
	county_modifier = {
		development_growth_factor = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_3
		monthly_county_control_change_factor = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_3
	}
	ai_value = {
		base = 15
	}
}

		OR = {
			has_building_or_higher = castle_01
			has_building_or_higher = tribe_01
		}

	}

	construction_time = standard_construction_time
	next_building = MA_sahelian_secular_06
	can_construct_potential = {
		has_building_or_higher = castle_03
		scope:holder.culture = { MA_aesthetic_tradition = { TRADITION = african } }
	}
	can_construct = { required_innovation = { INNOVATION = hoardings } }
	is_enabled = { scope:holder.capital_province = this }

		MA_medium_prestige_increase_effect = yes
		#Heavenly Vault perk
		MA_heavenly_vault_renown_effect = yes
	}
	character_modifier = {

	max_garrison = normal_building_max_garrison_tier_5

	cost_gold = normal_building_tier_1_cost
	construction_time = standard_construction_time
	next_building = MA_sahelian_religious_02
	can_construct_potential = {
		OR = {
			has_building_or_higher = castle_01
			has_building_or_higher = tribe_01
		}
		required_innovation = { INNOVATION = sahelian_art }
	}
	can_construct = { required_innovation = { INNOVATION = crop_rotation } }
	is_enabled = { required_religious_family = { FAMILY = pagan } is_county_capital = yes }
	on_complete = {
		MA_medium_development_increase_effect = yes
		MA_medium_piety_increase_effect = yes
		MA_patronage_perk_3_bonus = { TIER = 1 }
	}
	character_modifier = {
		clergy_opinion = 3
		monthly_piety_gain_mult = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
	}
	province_modifier = {
		build_speed = normal_building_build_speed_tier_1
		monthly_income = normal_building_tax_tier_1

	county_modifier = {
		development_growth_factor = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_3
		monthly_county_control_change_factor = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_3

	cost_gold = normal_building_tier_1_cost
	construction_time = standard_construction_time
	next_building = MA_tibetan_secular_02
	can_construct_potential = {
		has_building_or_higher = castle_01
		required_innovation = { INNOVATION = tibetan_art }
	}
	can_construct = { required_innovation = { INNOVATION = motte } }
	is_enabled = { scope:holder.capital_province = this }
	on_complete = {
		MA_medium_development_increase_effect = yes
		MA_medium_prestige_increase_effect = yes
		#Heavenly Vault perk
		MA_heavenly_vault_renown_effect = yes
	}

		direct_vassal_opinion = 3
		monthly_prestige_gain_mult = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
	}
	max_garrison = normal_building_max_garrison_tier_1
	province_modifier = {
		monthly_income = normal_building_tax_tier_1
	}
	county_modifier = {
		tax_mult = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
		levy_size = building_garrison_reinforcement_factor_tier_1
	}
	ai_value = {
		base = 15
	}
